2026-03-15T12:45:18.8809815Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8810224Z     ## 1. DESCRIÇÃO DO PROJECTO
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8810607Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8811266Z     **O que é:** mod para GTA San Andreas (PC, versão 1.0 US) que substitui o comportamento
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8812418Z     "ímã" dos companheiros de gangue por **IA veicular real**. O recruta dirige por conta própria,
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8813420Z     segue o jogador em carro, navega no road-graph nativo do motor RenderWare, desvia de
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8814267Z     obstáculos e mantém distância de segurança.
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8814726Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8815291Z     **Problema no jogo vanilla:** recrutas simplesmente teleportam ou correm em linha recta
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8816382Z     para o jogador — sem lógica de rua, sem desvio de carros, sem respeito ao trânsito.
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8817042Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8817315Z     **Stack:**
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8817993Z     - **GTA SA 1.0 US** — executável original sem patches
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8818707Z     - **CLEO 4** — scripting via opcodes RenderWare nativos
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8819390Z     - **Sanny Builder 3** — compilador de scripts CLEO
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8820214Z     - **DK22Pac/plugin-sdk** — SDK C++ para criar ficheiros `.asi` (DLLs nativas)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8821045Z     - **ASI Loader** — injector de DLLs no processo do jogo
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8821834Z     - **Visual Studio** — compilação do ASI (MSVC, Win32, Release/Debug)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8822618Z     - **Repositório:** `Reinoso-Pilado/tentativa1` (GitHub)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8823126Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8823398Z     ---
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8823672Z

2026-03-15T12:45:18.8930616Z     ## 5. BUGS DESCOBERTOS E ESTADO DE RESOLUÇÃO
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8930894Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8931199Z     ### 5.1 Bug Crítico: Recruta Congelado (on-foot, NÃO RESOLVIDO)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8931517Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8931847Z     **Sintoma:** recruta spawna, fica parado (task=203=STAND_STILL), nunca segue o jogador.
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8932429Z     `TellGroupToStartFollowingPlayer` é chamado 15+ vezes sem efeito.
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8932782Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8932985Z     **Causa raiz descoberta pelos logs:**
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8933506Z     1. `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup(g_recruit)` falha silenciosamente (**SEMPRE**, mesmo com pedType=8 e respect=1000)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8934275Z     2. `AddFollower` backup adiciona o ped ao array do grupo mas NÃO configura o Decision Maker (DM)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8935517Z     3. Sem DM configurado, `TellGroupToStartFollowingPlayer` → `CPedGroupDefaultTaskAllocatorFollowAnyMeans::CreateFirstSubTask` (0x666160) → **no-op**
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8936496Z     4. Task fica em 400 (desconhecida, possivelmente walk/spawn AI) e depois cai para 203 (STAND_STILL)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8936947Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8937268Z     **Hipótese principal (não confirmada, aguarda PRE_JOIN log):**
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8938865Z     O ped spawna como PED_TYPE_GANG2 (=8, GSF). GTA SA automaticamente coloca GSF NPCs em grupos de gang internos. Quando tentamos adicionar ao grupo do jogador (CPedGroups::ms_groups[0]), o jogo recusa porque o ped já pertence a outro grupo slot.
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8939805Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8939995Z     **Fix tentado e FALHOU:**
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8940801Z     - Boost de respeito **persistente** para 1000 (`ActivateRespectBoost`) — não ajudou porque ficava activo entre frames, causando efeitos HUD/gameplay, e não resolvia o DM.
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8941787Z     - Alterar pedType=GANG1→GANG2 — ajudou a não ser tratado como inimigo mas não resolveu o freeze
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8942388Z     - 5 bugs de spawn sequence corrigidos — não resolveram o freeze
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8942714Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8943118Z     **Fix IMPLEMENTADO (boost transiente — diferente do boost persistente anterior):**
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8943707Z     O boost persistente (`ActivateRespectBoost`) falhava porque ficava activo entre frames.
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8944363Z     O fix correcto é um **boost transiente**: aplicar STAT_RESPECT=1000 imediatamente antes de
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8945050Z     `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup` e restaurar logo após (dentro do mesmo frame, antes do próximo tick).
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8945718Z     Isto garante que `FindMaxGroupMembers() > 0` apenas no momento crítico do join, sem
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8946299Z     efeitos HUD ou de gameplay. Constante `RESPECT_BOOST_LEVEL=1000.0f` em grove_recruit_config.h.
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8946734Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8946900Z     ```cpp
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8947219Z     // Endereço da função interna: CreateFirstSubTask(0x666160)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8947851Z     // OU: usar CPed::GetIntelligence()->AddTaskComplexGangFollower(player)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8948476Z     // OU: encontrar endereço de CTaskComplexGangFollower::ctor e atribuir directamente
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8948871Z     ```
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8949036Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8949404Z     **Prova de diagnóstico esperada no próximo log (com PRE_JOIN + TASK_CHANGE):**
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8949781Z     ```
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8950055Z     PRE_JOIN: ped_em_grupo=X(slot=Y) FindMaxGroupMembers=Z respect=1000
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8950505Z     TASK_CHANGE: 400 -> 203  (spawn AI -> stand still, TellGroup foi no-op)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8950968Z     POST_FOLLOW_CHECK(3fr): activeTask=203 (PROBLEMA: TellGroup foi no-op)
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8951329Z     ```
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8951499Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8951665Z     ---

2026-03-15T12:45:18.8957286Z     1. **targetH constante:** `ClipTargetOrientationToLink` devolve sempre ≈2.55 rad. Não actualiza conforme o carro avança. **NÃO RESOLVIDO.**

2026-03-15T12:45:18.8961289Z     4. **speedMult sempre 1.00:** `m_nStraightLineDistance=20` fixo — não actualiza com distância real. **NÃO RESOLVIDO.**
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8961794Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8962035Z     **Comportamento por modo após fixes:**

2026-03-15T12:45:18.8969037Z     
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8969450Z     `m_fSeparationRange` (+0x30 em CPedGroup) era interpretado como ponteiro para `CPedGroupIntelligence*`.
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8970015Z     Escrever `100.0f = 0x42C80000` causava crash em `0x42C8021C`.
2026-03-15T12:45:18.8970595Z     **Fix:** usar `m_groupMembership.m_fMaxSeparation` (+0x2C). — Resolvido em commit `8a2d3a9`.

2026-03-15T12:45:18.8974891Z

2026-03-15T12:45:18.8976703Z     causando DismissRecruit automático.

2026-03-15T12:45:44.7256845Z     unsigned char AdaptiveSpeed(CVehicle* veh, float targetHeading, unsigned char baseSpeed)
2026-03-15T12:45:44.7257783Z     {

2026-03-15T12:45:44.7258505Z

2026-03-15T12:45:44.7262801Z         else if (absDH <= WRONG_DIR_THRESHOLD_RAD)

2026-03-15T12:45:44.7264195Z                    (WRONG_DIR_THRESHOLD_RAD - MISALIGNED_THRESHOLD_RAD) * CURVE_SPEED_REDUCTION;

2026-03-15T12:51:16.5644112Z 
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5651214Z I'm also noticing a pattern where the recruit might be cycling rapidly between FLEE and STAND_STILL states, so adding detection for that would help identify if it's stuck in a loop. For the driving problem at close range, the project notes suggest replacing CIVICO with GOTOCOORDS updated each frame using an offset behind the player, which would force road-following behavior even when nearby—but that's a bigger refactor than I can tackle without more context right now. I'm considering a few approaches: keeping the NPC at very low speed when the player gets close in CIVICO mode to prevent the chase behavior, or using a cruise mission with a waypoint ahead. But the real solution is probably to leverage the road-following system by setting a distant waypoint through GOTOCOORDS, since MISSION_43 switches to direct pursuit at close range and that's what's breaking the road adherence. to a "catch up" mode that uses direct navigation. The only way to prevent this is to either not use MISSION_43 at close range, or set a waypoint far away instead of the player's current position.
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5657918Z 
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5659509Z If I set the destination to a point ahead of the player along their heading and use GOTOCOORDS, that would force road-following at all distances, but it would need proper road-graph computation. Without JoinCarWithRoadSystem, GOTOCOORDS might not follow roads either.
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5661088Z 
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5667579Z The real issue is probably that the GTA SA engine switches MISSION_43 from road-following to direct approach when the recruit gets too close—maybe under 15 meters—and that's engine-level behavior I can't control directly. I could temporarily switch to MISSION_STOP_FOREVER with low speed when close, then switch back when the player moves away, which would make the recruit wait instead of chasing off-road. But wait, I'm already doing something similar with STOP_ZONE at 6m and SLOW_ZONE at 10m, so the issue must be happening at larger distances than expected. So the real issue is that when the recruit gets close—within about 20-30 meters—MISSION_43's close-approach behavior overrides the road-graph navigation and sends it chasing directly at the player. The fix would be to introduce a medium-range zone where, once the recruit enters it, we switch to a different mission like MISSION_STOP_FOREVER or MISSION_CRUISE to keep it following the roads instead of breaking off into a direct chase.
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5673070Z 
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5674638Z Looking at WRONG_DIR_RECOVERY, I see it's checking if the recruit is within a certain distance threshold and in Civico mode while the player is in a vehicle—when that condition triggers, it calls SetupDriveMode to recalibrate the driving behavior.
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5676135Z 
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5678740Z The problem is that SetupDriveMode invokes JoinCarWithRoadSystem, which re-snaps the vehicle to the road network. But if the recruit is approaching the player head-on and gets snapped to the road it came from, it ends up pointing away from the player instead. This creates a feedback loop where WRONG_DIR gets detected, recovery tries to fix it by re-snapping, but the snap puts it on the wrong road again, causing the recruit to drive erratically at close range.
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5681350Z 
2026-03-15T12:51:16.5685037Z The fix would be to either disable or tighten the WRONG_DIR_RECOVERY trigger to prevent this cycling behavior. I've identified the root cause: `GroupIntelComputeDefaultTasks` is being called with `g_recruit` instead of `player`, which is why FOLLOW_FALLBACK isn't triggering. Beyond that, I need to add task IDs 900, 501, and 502 to the logging, include the decision maker type in diagnostics, and update the log header. For the driving behavior, the WRONG_DIR recovery at close range might be causing incorrect re-snapping, so I should either remove it or make it distance-aware, and potentially add a medium zone between slow and open road to suppress the close-approach behavior from MISSION_43.

2026-03-15T12:53:20.4501190Z 
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4502367Z 1. **WRONG_DIR events at close range (10-30m)**: ALL the WRONG_DIR_START events are followed by WRONG_DIR_RECOVER (SetupDriveMode called) because they all occur when dist < 30m. This is happening a lot:
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4503955Z    - dist=10.0m, 20.7m, 21.8m, 13.5m, 22.6m, 13.5m, 11.5m
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4504493Z    
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4505244Z    The WRONG_DIR events have physSpeed=0-58 kmh, so sometimes the car is actually moving when WRONG_DIR starts.
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4506140Z    
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4508385Z 2. **The chase loop**: When the recruit approaches within 30m, WRONG_DIR triggers and SetupDriveMode resets the autopilot direction, creating a repeating cycle where the recruit gets close, loses orientation, re-snaps to a new heading, and starts approaching again—this is what produces the erratic chasing behavior.
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4509813Z 
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4511120Z 3. **WRONG_DIR persistence**: The duration of these wrong direction states varies wildly—most last under 2 seconds, but some stretch to 38-39 seconds, suggesting that after WRONG_DIR_RECOVER is called, the state sometimes fails to clear properly and lingers for extended periods.
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4512318Z 
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4513539Z 4. **Root cause analysis**: When WRONG_DIR_RECOVER triggers SetupDriveMode at very close range (10-30m), the JoinCarWithRoadSystem snap often selects a road node that causes the MISSION_43 engine to navigate backward relative to the actual road layout, creating these prolonged wrong-direction sequences.
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4514736Z 
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4515351Z The fix would be to avoid calling WRONG_DIR_RECOVER at such close distances—increasing the threshold to trigger only at greater ranges where the snap is more reliable.
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4515973Z 
2026-03-15T12:53:20.4517797Z Looking at the current logic, SetupDriveMode gets called whenever distance is under 30m, but I should add a minimum distance check to prevent the snap from happening when the recruit is already too close to the target. fires at close range, and the re-snap at close range causes the vehicle to navigate in the wrong direction for a long time (38+ seconds). The issue might be that `GetSimplestActiveTask` is traversing the task slots and returning a different task before reaching the follower task in slot 3.
2026-03-15T13:01:24.4167978Z 
2026-03-15T13:01:24.4171185Z Actually, I think I see it now—when `TellGroupToStartFollowingPlayer` creates the GANG_FOLLOWER task (1207) in slot 3, the engine simultaneously creates a physical response task (900) in an earlier slot. Since `GetSimplestActiveTask` returns the first non-null leaf task it finds while traversing slots 0 through 4, it hits task 900 before ever reaching 1207, which then cascades into the FLEE task (902). So the follower task exists but gets masked by this immediate engine response.
2026-03-15T13:01:24.4174059Z 
2026-03-15T13:01:24.4176759Z After FLEE ends, I'm wondering if the issue is that slot 3 gets cleared during the event cleanup, and since `bKeepTasksAfterCleanUp` might not be preserving it properly, the recruit defaults back to STAND_STILL (203) in slot 4 instead of resuming the follower behavior. KeepTasksAfterCleanUp means "don't clean up tasks after they're done". But FLEE is in slot[1] (EVENT_TEMP), and when FLEE ends, the task manager might clean up slot[1] and also slot[3] (the primary task) if they were conflicting.
2026-03-15T13:01:24.4179663Z 
2026-03-15T13:01:24.4186451Z Actually, I think the real issue is that task 900 in slot[0] triggers a FLEE response (902) in slot[1], which then cancels the GANG_FOLLOWER task (1207) sitting in slot[3] during its processing. Once FLEE ends and slot[1] clears, slot[3] is already gone—only STAND_STILL remains in slot[4]. So the question is what's creating task 900 in the first place. I'm looking at how the bRunning parameter affects task allocation - it seems to control follow speed rather than the allocator type itself, which always gets set to GangFollower. This makes me reconsider whether the issue is actually the bKeepTasksAfterCleanUp flag preventing the follow task from being assigned properly in the first place. manager might not allow new tasks to be assigned if the existing tasks haven't been cleaned up. If bKeepTasksAfterCleanUp=1 prevents cleanup, then when ComputeDefaultTasks tries to assign GANG_FOLLOWER to slot[3], it can't because the slot isn't cleared, so the assignment fails and the slot remains unchanged until it naturally empties—but by then the burst window has closed.
2026-03-15T13:01:24.4192735Z

2026-03-15T13:01:24.4201013Z 
2026-03-15T13:01:24.4203643Z If that's right, then ComputeDefaultTasks(g_recruit) should be correct for making g_recruit follow. With allocator type 4 (FollowLeaderAnyMeans), it creates the physical follow response in slot[0], whereas allocator type 1 (GangFollower) would create task 1207 in slot[3] if the respect check passes.
2026-03-15T13:01:24.4206202Z

2026-03-15T13:08:06.2063252Z       ## Summary of Changes
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2063633Z       
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2064020Z       This PR fixes two main bugs found by thoroughly reading the full grove_recruit.log:
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2064420Z       
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2064673Z       ### Bug 1: Frozen recruit on spawn (on-foot follow never works)
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2066203Z       - **Root cause**: `GroupIntelComputeDefaultTasks(pIntel, g_recruit)` was passing the **recruit** as arg. The function iterates group members and **skips the arg-ped** (skip-self behaviour) — so passing `g_recruit` caused the function to skip the only member that needed a follow task.
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2068240Z       - **Fix** (`grove_recruit_ai.cpp`, `grove_recruit_group.cpp`): Changed to `GroupIntelComputeDefaultTasks(pIntel, player)` so the recruit is processed and receives the follow task.
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2069255Z       
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2069574Z       ### Bug 2: Close-range "chase" driving (recruit goes off-road when near player)
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2071100Z       - **Root cause**: `WRONG_DIR_RECOVER` called `SetupDriveMode` when `dist < 30m`. This triggered `JoinCarWithRoadSystem` at close range, snapping to a wrong road node → recruit drove in the wrong direction for 38+ seconds (the "chase mode" seen in logs).
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2073832Z       - **Fix** (`grove_recruit_drive.cpp`): Inverted the condition from `dist < 30m` to `dist > 30m`. Now SetupDriveMode only fires when recruit is FAR from the player (where re-snapping is safe). Close range uses the periodic road snap (every 3s) instead.
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2075006Z       
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2075421Z       ### Log improvements (log upgrade as requested)

2026-03-15T13:08:06.2078206Z       - Updated log header to document all new findings (CLEO 0850 note, ComputeDefaultTasks skip-self bug, WRONG_DIR_RECOVER inversion, task 207/208/243 as valid follow states)
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2079866Z       - `POST_FOLLOW_CHECK` now accepts tasks 207/208/243 as valid follow states (in addition to 1207/1500)
2026-03-15T13:08:06.2081104Z       - Task 900 added as transient (same as 902/400) — avoids spurious FALLBACK triggers

2026-03-15T13:09:54.8532649Z copilot: ## Resumo das mudanças
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8533001Z 
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8533342Z ### Bug 1 — Recruta congelado no spawn (on-foot)
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8533726Z 
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8536130Z **Causa raiz confirmada pelo log**: `GroupIntelComputeDefaultTasks(pIntel, g_recruit)` estava passando o **próprio recruta** como argumento. A função itera os membros do grupo e **pula o ped-arg** (comportamento "skip-self"). Passar `g_recruit` fazia a função pular o único membro que precisava receber a task de follow — slot[3] ficava sempre `NO_TASK`.
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8538438Z 
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8539846Z **Fix** (`grove_recruit_group.cpp` + `grove_recruit_ai.cpp`): Mudado para `GroupIntelComputeDefaultTasks(pIntel, player)`. Agora o recruta é processado pela função e recebe a task de follow corretamente.
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8541133Z 
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8541432Z ### Bug 2 — Modo "chase" quando próximo do jogador
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8541802Z 
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8543777Z **Causa raiz confirmada pelo log**: `WRONG_DIR_RECOVER` chamava `SetupDriveMode` quando `dist < 30m`. O `JoinCarWithRoadSystem` em range próximo snappava para um nó de estrada com orientação errada → recruta dirigia na direção errada por **38+ segundos consecutivos** = o "modo chase" off-road.
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8545847Z 
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8547199Z **Fix** (`grove_recruit_drive.cpp`): Condição invertida de `dist < 30m` para `dist > 30m`. Agora só faz re-snap quando longe (seguro). Range próximo usa o snap periódico (a cada 3s).
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8548407Z 
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8548539Z ### Log upgrade
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8548715Z 
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8548963Z - **9 novos IDs de task**: 205, 207, 208, 243, 501, 502, 719, 806, 813, 900
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8549995Z - Task 207/208/243 explicadas: são estados de follow válidos — `POST_FOLLOW_CHECK` agora aceita-as (além de 1207/1500)
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8550975Z - Task 900 = react-to-command de 1 frame (transitório, como 902/400)
2026-03-15T13:09:54.8551766Z - Header atualizado com todos os achados (nota sobre CLEO 0850, bug skip-self, WRONG_DIR invertido)

2026-03-15T13:10:18.0295711Z Recruit consistently freezes on foot after spawn (never reaches task 1207/follow state), and in CIVICO mode drives off-road/sidewalks when close to the player instead of following road graph.
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0296427Z 
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0296544Z ## Root causes identified via full log analysis
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0296754Z 
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0297194Z ### Bug 1 — `ComputeDefaultTasks` skip-self: frozen recruit
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0299491Z `CPedGroupIntelligence::ComputeDefaultTasks(0x5F88D0)` iterates group members and **skips the ped passed as argument**. Both FALLBACK and AddFollower-backup paths were passing `g_recruit`, causing the function to silently skip the only member that needed a follow task — `slot[3]` stayed `NO_TASK` every cycle.
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0301474Z 
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0301605Z ```cpp
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0302160Z // Before (bug): recruit is the arg → skipped → no task assigned
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0302832Z GroupIntelComputeDefaultTasks(pIntel, g_recruit);
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0303084Z 
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0303359Z // After: player (leader) is the arg → recruit is processed → receives follow task
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0303793Z GroupIntelComputeDefaultTasks(pIntel, player);
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0304070Z ```
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0304168Z 
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0304483Z Fixed in both `grove_recruit_group.cpp` (AddFollower backup path) and `grove_recruit_ai.cpp` (FOLLOW_FALLBACK).
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0304898Z 
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0305100Z ### Bug 2 — `WRONG_DIR_RECOVER` at close range: chase behavior
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0306216Z `WRONG_DIR_RECOVER` fired `SetupDriveMode` (→ `JoinCarWithRoadSystem`) when `dist < 30m`. At close range this snapped to a wrong road node, putting the recruit in WRONG_DIR for **38+ seconds consecutively** — the observed off-road "chase mode".
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0307040Z 
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0307115Z ```cpp
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0307603Z // Before: fires at close range, bad snap → 38s wrong-navigation
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0307988Z if (dist < WRONG_DIR_RECOVERY_DIST_M && ...)
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0308185Z 
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0308392Z // After: fires only when far (>30m), safe to re-snap; close range uses periodic snap
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0308807Z if (dist > WRONG_DIR_RECOVERY_DIST_M && ...)
2026-03-15T13:10:18.0309059Z ```
